梵文：namaḥ samanta buddhānāṃ  oṃ  bhrūṃ
音译：那麻ḥ 萨曼塔 布达囊 嗡 布隆


M01.02卍一切如来部母佛眼陀罗尼卍
梵文：namaḥ sarva tathā gate bhyo  rha bhyaḥ  samya ksaṃ buddhe bhyaḥ  oṃ  ruru  sphuru  jvala  tiṣṭha  siddha locani  sarva artha sadhane  svāhā
音译：那麻 萨瓦 塔塔嘎帖 贝友 阿尔哈帖贝友 桑雅克桑 布帖贝友 嗡 汝汝 斯普汝 及瓦拉 谛瑟塔 悉达 洛佳尼 萨尔瓦 阿尔塔 萨达内 斯瓦哈

hārā  gandhā hārā  puṣpa hārā  phalā hārā  sasya hāra  pāpa cittā  duṣṭa cittā  raudra citta  yakṣa graha  rākṣasa graha  preta graha  piśaca graha  bhūta graha  kumbhaṇḍa graha  skanda graha  utmāda graha  cchāya graha  apasmāra graha  ḍākaḍakinī graha  revati graha  jamika graha  śakuni graha  matra nandika graha  lamvika graha  hanu kaṇṭha pāṇi graha  jvara ekahika  dvetiyaka  straitī yaka  catu rthaka  nitya jvarā  viṣama jvara  vātikā paittika  śleṣmika  sanni patika  sarva jvara  śirortti  ardhava bhe daka  arocaka  akṣirogaṃ  nasa rogaṃ  mukha rogaṃ  hṛdrogaṃ  gala grahaṃ  karṇa śūlaṃ  danta śūlaṃ  hṛdaya śūlaṃ  marma śulaṃ  pārṣva śūlaṃ  pṛṣṭhaśūlaṃ  udara śūlaṃ  kaṇti śūlaṃ  vasti śūlaṃ  ūruśūlaṃ  jāṅghaśulaṃ  hastaśūlaṃ  pādaśūlaṃ  sarvaṅga pratyaṅgaśūlaṃ  bhūta vetāḍa  ḍākaḍākinī  jvara  dadru kāṇḍu  kiṭibha lūta vai  sarpa luhāliṅga  śoṣatra  sagara viṣa yoga  agni udaka  para vaira kāntāra  akālaṃ mṛtyu  traimuka  trailaṭaka  vṛścika  sarpa nakula  siṃgha vyāghra  ṛkṣa tarakṣu  mṛga  svapara jiva  teṣāṃ sarveṣaṃ  sittatapatraṃ  mahā vajro ṣṇīṣaṃ  mahā pratyaṅgiraṃ  yavadva daśayo jāna bhyantareṇa  simā bandhaṅkaromi  diśabandhaṅkaromi  pāravidyā bandhaṅkaromi  tejo bandhaṅkaromi  hasta bandhaṅkaromi  pada bandhaṅkaromi  sarvaṅga pratyaṅga bandhaṅkaromi  tadyathā  oṃ  anale anale  viśade viśade  vera vajra dhare  bandha bandhani  vajrapāṇi  phaṭ  hūṃ  trūṃ  phaṭ  svāhā  namaḥ stathā gatāya  sugatayārhate  samya ksaṃ buddhaya  siddhyantu mantrapada  svāhā

M03.16卍金刚手说佛心陀罗尼(佛心陀罗尼)卍
梵文：namo bhagavato vajra paṇaye  guhya kādhi pataye  tadyathā  hihi vajrapaṇi  hehe vajra paṇi  hī hī vajrapaṇi  kili kili vajra paṇi  kuru kuru śabdena  dhara dhara  kili kili  hana hana vajreṇa  hihi hihi  hini hini  rāva rāva  nīlamvaradhara vajrapaṇi  hiri hiri  kiri kiri  vajravajra vajravajra  vajrāṭṭahasa  kuru kuru  kulu kulu  kumbhaṇḍāṃ trasaya vajreṇa  martha martha  udālaya vajreṇa  vajrakāla kalaṃ  para para  huṃ huṃ huṃ huṃ  phaṭ phaṭ  trāsaya vajreṇa  hana hana  kaḍha kaḍha  trasaya vajreṇa  matha matha bhramaya  kara kara  laghu laghu  kākā kīkī  kuru kuru  bhagavaṃ vajra kāla  para para  hana hana  kulutsādanaṃ  kuru kuru  kṛṣṇa śavara piśacā dhi pataye  ehi miri vajra  miri kiri vajra  kiri tiri vajra  tiri viri vajra  viri śavari vajra  śavara varma vajra  ībhū nirbhū tabhū  miri mari  kṛṣṇa śavara śavari piśacā dhipataye  kuru kuru guhya kādhi pataye  piri piri caṇḍa vajrakāla  divyakanana  rājata vajra vaiḍūrya  mukti kāñcanā laṅkṛtā bharaṇa  bhaṇḍa bhaṇḍa  gaccha gaccha  nivedaya  śīghraṃ vajracihna  laghu laghu  jalpāpaya kelapaya  kampapaya  kiṭi moṭapaya  raṅgāpaya  trasaya  samohaya  bhramaya bhramaya vajreṇa  vajracaṇḍa  caṇḍa graha  ākuṭaya ākāśaṃ stambhaya  divyaṃ stambhaya  nāgagrahaṇa  yakṣa grahaṇa  sarva duṣṭa grahaṇāṃ  paca pācaya  stambhaya  bandha bandha ciri ciri  bhara bhara  pūra pūra  pūrapaya vajreṇa  apasmāra grahaṃ āveśaya  cara cara  para para  pūrapaya pūrapaya vajreṇa  vighnaṃ hana hana  vitrāsaya  akaḍha akaḍha  vajrā kuśena  dhiri dhiri  skandha grahaṃ utsadaya  bhagavāṃ vajrapaṇi  karmame kuru kuru  muru muru  huru huru  ārya siddha ścaṇḍa vajrapaṇi rājña payati  svāhā

梵文：oṃ  padma  cakra  śaṅkha  gada  dhāraṇi  nīlakaṇṭha  siddhya siddhya  hūṃ

M16.02卍最胜明王真言(不空羂索最胜明王陀罗尼)卍
梵文：nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva buddha bodhi satve bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddhā rya śravaka saṅghe bhyo  titana gata pratyu tpanne bhyaḥ  namaḥ samya ggatanāṃ  namaḥ samya kprati pannanāṃ  namaḥ śāra dvatī sutāya mahā mataye  namaḥ ārya maitreya pra mukhe bhyo  mahā bodhi satva ārya gaṇa vare bhyo  namo amitā bhaya tathā gatāyā  rhate samya ksaṃ buddhāya  namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  ebhyo mahā iṛṣi ārya gaṇa vare bhyo  nama skṛtvenāṃ  āryā valokite śvara  mukhu dgī rṇa  mamo gha rājāṃ  nāma hṛdayaṃ  tathā gata saṃ mukha bhā ṣitaṃ  mahā tpa rṣa madhye  ahami dānī  māvartta iṣyāmi  siddhya ntume  sarva kāryāṇi  sarva bhaye ṣucame  rakṣa bhavatu  tadyathā  oṃ  cara cara  ciri ciri  curu curu  mahā kāru ṇikāya  viri viri  piri piri  ciri ciri  parama kāru ṇikā  siri siri  piri piri  ciri ciri  mahā padma hastāya  kala kala  kili kili  kulu kulu  mahā śuddha satvāya  ehyehi  buddhya buddhya  dhava dhava  kaṇa kaṇa  kiṇi kiṇi  kuṇu kuṇu  parama śuddha satvāya  kara kara  kiri kiri  kuru kuru  mahā sthāma praptāya  cala cala  sañcala sañcala  vicala vicala  eṭaṭa eṭaṭa  bhara bhara  bhiri bhiri  bhuru bhuru  ehyehi  mahā karu ṇikā  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  sara sara  mara mara  cara cara  hara hara  hāhā hāhā  hīhī hīhī  huhu huhu  oṃ kara  brahma veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  dhiri dhiri  dhuru dhuru  tara tara  sara sara  para para  cara cara  vara vara  raśmi śata saha sra  pratima ṇḍita śarīra  jvala jvala  tapa tapa  bhagavaṃ  suma nitya  yama varuṇa kuvera  brahmi ndra  iṛṣide vagaṇa bhya rcitta caraṇa  suru suru  curu curu  puru puru  muru muru  sana tku mara  rudra vasāva  viṣṇu dhanada  deva iṛṣi nāyaka  bahu vivi dhaveṣa dhara  dhara dhara  dhiri dhiri  dhuru dhuru  thara thara  ghara ghara  yara yara  lara lara  hara hara  mara mara  para para  vara vara  vara dayaka  samantā valokita  vilokita  loke śvara  mahe śvara  muhu muhu  muru muru  muyu muyu  muñca muñca  bhaga vaṃ ārya valokite śvara  rakṣa rakṣa māṃ  sarva bhaye bhyaḥ  sarvo padrave bhyaḥ  sarvo pasarge bhyaḥ  sarvo pāyase bhyaḥ  sarva grahe bhyaḥ  sarva vyā dhi bhyaḥ  sarva vadha bandhana  rāja cora taskara  agnyu daka viṣa śastra  parimo caka  kaṇa kaṇa  kiṇi kiṇi  kuṇu kuṇu  cara cara  indriya  bala bodhiṃ ṅga  catu ārya satya saṃ praka śaka  tama tama  dama dama  sama sama  mahā tamo ndhakara  vidhamana  ṣa ṭpara mita  paripū raka  mili mili  ṭaṭa ṭaṭa  ṭhaṭha ṭhaṭha  ṭiṭi ṭiṭi  ṭhuṭhu ṭhuṭhu  eṇeya carma kṛta pari kara  ehyehi  īśvara  mahe śvara  mahā bhuta gaṇa bhañjaka  kuru kuru  para para  kara kara  kaṭa kaṭa  maṭa maṭa  viśuddha viṣaya vāsiṃ  mahā kāru ṇika  śveta yajṇo pavīta  ratna makuṭa mālā dhara  sarva jña śirasi kṛta  jaṭā makuṭa  mahā dbhuta  kamala kṛta  kara tala  dhyāna samā dhi vimo kṣa prakaṃ pya  bahu satva santati  paripā caka  mahā kāru ṇika  sarva karmā varaṇa viśo dhaka  sarva vyādhi pramo caka  sarvā śapari pūraka  sarva satva sama śvā saka  namo stute  svāhā

M16.03卍奋怒王真言(不空奋怒王陀罗尼)(最上不空奋怒王陀罗尼)卍
梵文：namaḥ sarva tathā gata  āryā valokite śvara  vajra dhare bhyaḥ  oṃ  cara cara  ciri ciri  curu curu  mahā kāru ṇika  ciri ciri  viri viri  mahā padma hasta  kala kala  kili kili  kulu kulu  mahā sthāma prapta  cara cara  cacara  niśacare śvara  ehyehi  siddhya siddhya  buddhya buddhya  dhava dhava  kiṇi kiṇi  parama śuddha satva  kara kara  kiri kiri  kuru kuru  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  hāhā hīhī hūhū  oṃ kara  brahma veṣa dhara  sara sara  vara vara  raśmi śata saha sra  pratima ṇḍita śarīra  jvala jvala  tapa tapa  bhagavaṃ  suma nitya yama varuṇa kuvera  brahmi ndra  iṛṣi deva gaṇa  bhya rcitta caraṇa  suru suru  muru muru  sana tku māra  rudra vasava  dhanada  deva iṛṣi nāyaka  bahu vivi dha veṣa dhara  dhara dhara  samantā valokita  vilokita loke śvara  mahe śvara  muyu muyu  muñca muñca  vadha bandhana  taḍana rājata skara  āgnyu daka  viṣa śastra  parimo caka  kaṇa kaṇa  bala bodhi ṅga  catu ārya satya  saṃ praka śaka  tama tama  sama sama  masa masa  mahā vidya ndhakara  praśamana  mili mili  eṇeya carma pari kara  ehyehi  maṭa maṭa  viśuddha viṣaya vasiṃ  mahā kāru ṇika  śveta yajṇo pavīta  ratna makuṭa mala dhara  sarva jña śirasi  kṛta kara puṭa  dhyāna sama dhi  vimo kṣa prakaṃ pya  ṣa ṭpara mita  pari pū raka  bahu satva santati  paripā caka  sarva mārani duṣṭa  pramardaka  sarva siddhyā śāpari pūraka  abhi ṣi ñca  sarva tathā gatā bhiṣeke  bhagavaṃ amogha rāja  hūṃ  phaṭ  namo stute  svāhā

M16.04卍悉地王真言(不空悉地王陀罗尼)卍
梵文：namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ ārya amitā bhāya tathā gatāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  tadyathā  oṃ  padme padme  padma dhara vibhu ṣita bhuje  cara cara  brahma veṣa dhara  bhara bhara  vicitra mauli dhara  maṇi kanaka  vajra vaiṇū ryā laṅkṛta śarīra  tara tara  taraya bhagavaṃ  bhagavati paraṃ  dhuru dhuru  amogha paśa hasta  vara vara  vara dayaka  samantā valokita  mahā bodhi satva varada  padma sāna  padma gaura  jvala jvala  sarva tathā gatā bhi ṣekā bhi ṣikta  mahā kāru ṇika  bala bala  mahā bala vega dhara  vikṛta nāna  daṃ ṣṭrā karala  mahā teja dhara  vipula jñana varada  mahā kāru ṇika  mahā paśu pati veṣa dhara  sara sara  prasara  puṇya saṃ bhara  sugata dhyana sama dhi  samantā valokita  īśvara  mahe śvara  duṣṭa damaka  raudra pralaya  damaka krodharāja  mahā vega dhara  sama sama  mahā sthāma prapta  candra sūrya  trika prabha  mala mala  sarva mala viśo dhaka  sarva iṛṣi gaṇa santati  mahā mahe śvara rūpa dhara  amitā bhaji nālaṅkṛta  jaṭā dakṣiṇa  candra laṅkṛta śira  matha matha  sarva yakṣa rakṣasa  bhūta gaṇa bhañjaka  tara tara  tara gaṇa samalaṅkṛta  dakṣa tra mara  sarva vighna vinā śana kara  parama maitra citta  mahā kāru ṇika  para para  pari pūrṇa maṇḍala  sau mya mukha  ṣa ṭpāra mita pari pūraka  miri miri  eṇeya carma  vasāna vya ghra carmo tarya  dhara dhara  sarva tathā gatā valokita  trine tra  triśula dhara  vajra jvala dhara  amogha pāśa hasta  yama varuṇa  kuvera rūpa dhara  nagi ndra rūpa dhara  vimala viśo dhaneha  sarva papa praśamaka  sarvā varaṇa viśo dhaka  sarva kilviṣa naśaka  tre lokya vaśaṅkara  sarva satva viśo dhaka  bodhi bodhi  bodhi satva varada  sarva tathā gatā dhiṣṭhite  oṃ  padma vibhu ṣita śuddhe  dhiri dhiri  āva lokaya māṃ  sama sama  sarva karma vesā dhaya  amogha paśa hṛdaya  siddhe guhya  deva sini  varada  hūṃ  phaṭ  namo stute  svāhā

M19.02卍清净莲华明王央俱舍真言(清净莲花明王央俱舍陀罗尼)卍
梵文：nama strya dhva nugata  prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  sarva buddha bodhi satva  prasara tathā gata guhya  maṇḍala mudrā mantra  prasara samu dre bhyaḥ  namaḥ ārya vajra dhara  sarva kula guhya vidyā dhari ndra prati ṣṭhite bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva pratyeka buddhā rya śrā vaka saṅghe bhyo  tīta nagata pratyu tpanne bhyaḥ  namaḥ sarva maṇḍala guhya  mahā vidyā rāja sadhana siddhe bhyaḥ  namo ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valo kite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  sarva vidyā maṇḍala rāja  mahā mogha vikurvaṇa siddhe bhyaḥ  sarva mudre bhyaḥ  tadyathā  oṃ  vimale  vimala garbhe  vimalāṃ muja padme  surya varcase  saha sra raśmi kiraṇe  mahā raśmi jvalā vabha site  cara cara  cacara  sañcara  padmo tari  padma garbhe  padma bhuje  suni rmalaṃ muja vimale  maṇi kanaka  vajra vai ḍuri ndra nīla mara kata  padma rāga  vivi dhamahā maṇi  ratnālaṅkṛta śarire  dhara dhara  mahā padma dhare  para para  paraśu paśadhare  sara sara  samanta vairo cana  sarva tathā gata guhyā dhiṣṭhite  kula samayaṃ  pari pūraṇi  dhara dhara  vajra jvalā māla garbhe  vajra vajre  vajrā dhiṣṭhita padme  hūṃ hūṃ  maṇi maṇi  mahā maṇi  cinta maṇi paśadhara  huru huru  padme padme gaure  padma paṇi varade  amogha padme  oṃ  padmini  padma maṇi vajra dhare  sarva tathā gata kula sāmā nya  samayā dhiṣṭhite  mahā vipula bhuje  bhara bhara  saṃ bhara saṃ bhara  bhuru bhuru  bhu raṇi  bhiri bhiri  samantā valokita vidyā rāje  prasara prasara  samanta vimale  sarva vidyā maṇḍala devata  nama skṛte  tara tara  tāraya tāraya  samantāśā pari pūraṇi  sarva bodhi satvā bhiṣe cani  sarva tathā gatā moghā bhiṣikte  abhiṣi ñcaya māṃ  sarva vidyā maṇḍala  kula samayā bhiṣekeḥ  sarva tathā gata pāṇi varade  padma gauri  padma prabhe  padma vikajaṃ muja garbhe  hūṃ hūṃ  vajre vajre  vajra padme  tathā gata kulā dhiṣṭhite  amogha varade  sarvā śāpari pūraṇi  sarvā pāya duḥ kha praśamani  amogha hṛdaya siddhi  sādhaya vimale  hūṃ  phaṭ  oṃ  varade padma bhuje  namo stute  padma puṭe  svāhā

aśītīnāṃ naga saha sraṇāṃ  bhavanāṃ kampāpaya  huṃ huṃ phaṭ  viṣṇu mahe śvara sya  saputra sya  bhavanāṃ kampāpaya  huṃ huṃ phaṭ  gu hya kanāṃ  bhavanāṃ kampāpaya  huṃ huṃ phaṭ  bho bho  guhya kakiṃ tiṣṭhasi muñca ṭṭa hasaṃ  śivaṃ darśaya yatha malaṃ laṃ  huṃ huṃ phaṭ  bho bho kru dha sarva buddhanujñata  acintya bala para krama  akaḍha akaḍha  pataya pataya  śighraṃ śighraṃ  sarva deva nāga asura garuḍa  yakṣa rākṣasa  gandharva kinnara maho raga  kumbhaṇḍa piśaca utmadā  apa  smara  pūtana kaṭa pūtananāṃ  naśaya  rakṣa rakṣa mama  huṃ huṃ  phaṭ phaṭ phaṭ phaṭ phaṭ  saputra M25.13 卍金刚手大身陀罗尼(金刚手秘密主大身陀罗尼)卍

M27.18 卍大金刚忿怒王入解脱三摩地现大神通降伏三界诸天龙神陀罗尼(大金刚忿怒王降伏三界陀罗尼)卍

ratna trayāya  namaḥ āryā valokite śvarāya  bodhi satvāya  mahā satvāya  mahā kāru ṇikāya  namaḥ iśvara  mahe śvara rupā valokitāya  brahma viṣṇu mahe śvara  kumāra pramukhe bhyo deva putre bhyaḥ
